Varada V N A Santosh
Table of Contents
  • Vanilla Softmax Calculation but using Safe Softmax functio to avoid numeric overflow
  • Second Block of Q,K,V
  • Calculate L & M values for the current Block of $Q_{1}$ & $K_{1}$
  • Load Q2 Block and peform Dot Product Between (This is for each $K_{i}$ Block loaded in outerloop we perform the dot product with all the $Q_{j}$ Block)
  • Calculate Softmax for Dot Product between $Q_{2}$ & $K_{1}$
  • Calculate L & M for the Current Blocks of $Q_{2}$ & $K_{1}$
  • Let us merge the Q1_K1_SM & Q2_K2_SM Softmax Matrices to calculate the incremental Softmax
  • Below we are perorming few steps , let us try to understand them one by one
  • Now we are done with Performing Dot Product and Softmax calculations of Q Block with all the $K_{1}$ Blocks, we need to repeat the step for the $K_{2}$ blocks, hence we will load the $K_{2}$ Block from HBM onto Onchip Memory
  • Calculate the Softmax for $Q_{1}$ & $K_{2}$
  • Calculate L & M values for the current block of $Q_{1}$ & $K_{2}$
  • Calculate Softmax between $Q_{2}$ Block and $K_{2}$
  • Calculate the L & M for the current blocks Q2 & K2
  • Let us merge the Q1_K2_SM & Q2_K2_SM Softmax Matrices to calculate the incremental Softmax
  • Vanilla Softmax Attention Scores
  • Online Softmax Attention Scores 

import numpy as np

np.random.seed(42)
Q = np.arange(1,9).reshape(4,2)
K = np.arange(9,17).reshape(4,2)
V = np.arange(18,26).reshape(4,2)

Q,K,V

(array([[1, 2],
        [3, 4],
        [5, 6],
        [7, 8]]),
 array([[ 9, 10],
        [11, 12],
        [13, 14],
        [15, 16]]),
 array([[18, 19],
        [20, 21],
        [22, 23],
        [24, 25]]))

Q_K_VANILLA= np.dot(Q,K.T)

def safe_softmax(x):
  max = np.max(x)
  return np.exp(x-max)/np.sum(np.exp(x-max))

Vanilla Softmax Calculation but using Safe Softmax functio to avoid numeric overflow#

Q_K_VANILLA_SM = safe_softmax(Q_K_VANILLA)
Q_K_VANILLA_SM

array([[2.53469490e-89, 1.02256891e-86, 4.12533740e-84, 1.66427989e-81],
       [8.07450679e-73, 9.71043646e-67, 1.16778125e-60, 1.40437873e-54],
       [2.57220937e-56, 9.22114642e-47, 3.30570063e-37, 1.18506486e-27],
       [8.19401262e-40, 8.75651076e-27, 9.35762297e-14, 1.00000000e+00]])

Brief Overview of Flash Attention Algorithm

Load $K_{i}$,$V_{i}$ Blocks from HBM to On-Chip Memory in Outerloop (Repeat for All K,V Blocks)

  1. Load $Q_{j}$ , $O_{j}$ , $l_{j}$ , $m_{j}$ from HBM to On-Chip Memory in inner loop

  2. Calculate Dot product between Block of $K_{i}$ & $Q_{j}$ , this produces $S_{ij}$

  3. Calculate the Online Softmax on $S_{ij}$ using the formulae mentioned below, note these results are not correct , but we will get the final result after processing all the blocks using $l_{j}$ & $m_{j}$ which are required for calculating the online softmax

  4. Perform the dot product between result of Softmax with $V_{i}$ and store the result in $O_{j}$

  1. Finally Write $O_{j}$ , $l_{j}$ & $m_{j}$ to HBM Memory

Finally Return O, Which contains the final attention Score

Let us assume that we are dividing Q,K,V into 2 Blocks

#First Block of Q,K,V

Q_1 = Q[:2,:]
K_1 = K[:2,:]
V_1 = V[:2,:]
Q_1,K_1,V_1

(array([[1, 2],
        [3, 4]]),
 array([[ 9, 10],
        [11, 12]]),
 array([[18, 19],
        [20, 21]]))

Second Block of Q,K,V#

Q_2 = Q[2:,:]
K_2= K[2:,:]
V_2 =V[2:,:]
Q_2,K_2,V_2

(array([[5, 6],
        [7, 8]]),
 array([[13, 14],
        [15, 16]]),
 array([[22, 23],
        [24, 25]]))

For the time being We will not use V matrix in our calculation as we are trying to find if the Softmax Calculations are same after doing this batch of operations

#Load $K_{1}$ & $Q_{1}$ Blocks

Q1_K1 =  np.dot(Q_1,K_1.T)

#Calculate Softmax for the $Q_{1}$ & $K_{1}$

Q1_K1_SM  = safe_softmax(Q1_K1)

Calculate L & M values for the current Block of $Q_{1}$ & $K_{1}$#

Q1_K1_MAX = np.max(Q1_K1)
Q1_K1_L = np.sum(np.exp(Q1_K1-Q1_K1_MAX))

Load Q2 Block and peform Dot Product Between (This is for each $K_{i}$ Block loaded in outerloop we perform the dot product with all the $Q_{j}$ Block)#

Q2_K1 =  np.dot(Q_2,K_1.T)

Calculate Softmax for Dot Product between $Q_{2}$ & $K_{1}$#

Q2_K1_SM = safe_softmax(Q2_K1)

Calculate L & M for the Current Blocks of $Q_{2}$ & $K_{1}$#

Q2_K1_MAX = np.max(Q2_K1)
Q2_K1_L = np.sum(np.exp(Q2_K1-Q2_K1_MAX))

Let us merge the Q1_K1_SM & Q2_K2_SM Softmax Matrices to calculate the incremental Softmax#

Below we are perorming few steps , let us try to understand them one by one#

  1. as we are merging two blocks we need to compute the new maximum the value Q_K1_MAX in below is representing this

  2. While calculating the new Softmax the formula says as below [ $ e^ {m (x_{1}) - m(x)} \cdot f(x_{1}) $, $ e^ {m (x_{2}) - m(x)} \cdot f(x_{2}) $ ]

  3. $f(x_{1})$ = $e^ {(x_{1})-m (x_{1})}$/Σ$e^ {(x_{1})-m (x_{1})}$ & $f(x_{2})$ = $e^ {(x_{2})-m (x_{2})}$/$e^ {(x_{2})-m (x_{2})}$

  4. After multiplying the first batch softmax with $ e^ {m (x_{1}) - m(x)} , f(x_{1}) $ would be transformed to $e^ {(x_{1})-m (x)} $/Σ$e^ {(x_{1})-m (x_{1})}$ , similary second batch softmax needs to be multiplied with $ e^ {m (x_{2}) - m(x)}$ which transforms $f(x_{2})$ to
    $e^ {(x_{2})-m (x)} $/Σ$e^ {(x_{2})-m (x_{2})}$, these corresonds to the steps to Q1_K1_SM & Q2_K1_SM

  5. New L for the Batch merged needs to be calculated using $L_{1}$ & $L_{2}$, below is what happens when we perform these operations , Q_K1_L in below corresponds to calculation of new L

$L_{1}$ = Σ$e^ {(x_{1})-m (x_{1})}$ & $L_{2}$ = Σ$e^ {(x_{2})-m (x_{2})}$

L = $ e^ {m (x_{1}) - m(x)} \cdot L(x^{1})
$ + $ e^ {m (x_{2}) - m(x)} \cdot L(x^{2})
$

L= $ e^ {(x_{1}) - m(x)}
$ + $ e^ {(x_{2}) - m(x)}
$

  1. Last step in calculating the new softmax is $f(x)/l(x)$ , hence $f(x_{1})$ & $f(x_{2})$ calculted in step-4 would be divided by new L calculated in step-5, this would gives the final softmax for the blocks merged
Q_K1_MAX = max(np.max(Q1_K1_MAX),np.max(Q2_K1_MAX))
Q1_K1_SM = np.array(Q1_K1_SM) * np.exp(Q1_K1_MAX- Q_K1_MAX)* Q1_K1_L
Q2_K1_SM = np.array(Q2_K1_SM) * np.exp(Q2_K1_MAX- Q_K1_MAX) * Q2_K1_L
Q_K1_L = (np.exp(Q1_K1_MAX- Q_K1_MAX) * Q1_K1_L) + (np.exp(Q2_K1_MAX- Q_K1_MAX) * Q2_K1_L)
Q_K1_SM =np.vstack((Q1_K1_SM,Q2_K1_SM))
Q_K1_SM = Q_K1_SM/Q_K1_L
Q_K1_SM

array([[2.89464031e-63, 1.16778125e-60],
       [9.22114642e-47, 1.10893902e-40],
       [2.93748211e-30, 1.05306174e-20],
       [9.35762297e-14, 1.00000000e+00]])

Now we are done with Performing Dot Product and Softmax calculations of Q Block with all the $K_{1}$ Blocks, we need to repeat the step for the $K_{2}$ blocks, hence we will load the $K_{2}$ Block from HBM onto Onchip Memory#

Q1_K2 = np.dot(Q_1,K_2.T)

Calculate the Softmax for $Q_{1}$ & $K_{2}$#

Q1_K2_SM  = safe_softmax(Q1_K2)

Calculate L & M values for the current block of $Q_{1}$ & $K_{2}$#

Q1_K2_MAX = np.max(Q1_K2)
Q1_K2_L = np.sum(np.exp(Q1_K2-Q1_K2_MAX))

Load Q2 Block and peform Dot Product Between (This is for each Ki Block loaded in outerloop we perform the dot product with all the Qj Block) , Current Blocks we are processing are $Q_{2}$ & $K_{2}$

Q2_K2 = np.dot(Q_2,K_2.T)

Calculate Softmax between $Q_{2}$ Block and $K_{2}$#

Q2_K2_SM = safe_softmax(Q2_K2)

Calculate the L & M for the current blocks Q2 & K2#

Q2_K2_MAX = np.max(Q2_K2)
Q2_K2_L = np.sum(np.exp(Q2_K2-Q2_K2_MAX))

Let us merge the Q1_K2_SM & Q2_K2_SM Softmax Matrices to calculate the incremental Softmax#

Q_K2_MAX = max(np.max(Q1_K2_MAX),np.max(Q2_K2_MAX))
Q1_K2_SM = np.array(Q1_K2_SM) * np.exp(Q1_K2_MAX- Q_K2_MAX)*Q1_K2_L
Q2_K2_SM = np.array(Q2_K2_SM) * np.exp(Q2_K2_MAX- Q_K2_MAX)*Q2_K2_L
Q_K2_L = (np.exp(Q1_K2_MAX- Q_K2_MAX) * Q1_K2_L) + (np.exp(Q2_K2_MAX- Q_K2_MAX) * Q2_K2_L)
Q_K2_SM =np.vstack((Q1_K2_SM,Q2_K2_SM))
Q_K2_SM = Q_K2_SM/Q_K2_L
Q_K2_SM

array([[4.12533740e-84, 1.66427989e-81],
       [1.16778125e-60, 1.40437873e-54],
       [3.30570063e-37, 1.18506486e-27],
       [9.35762297e-14, 1.00000000e+00]])

#Finally Merge the Sotmax matrices Q_K1_SM & Q_K2_SM, this would be the final Soft matrix which should be the final, this softmax matrix values should be equivalent to the Vanilla Softmax attention values

Q_K_MAX = max(np.max(Q_K1_MAX),np.max(Q_K2_MAX))
Q_K1_SM =  Q_K1_SM * np.exp(Q_K1_MAX- Q_K_MAX) * Q_K1_L
Q_K2_SM =  Q_K2_SM * np.exp(Q_K2_MAX- Q_K_MAX) * Q_K2_L
Q_K_L = (np.exp(Q_K1_MAX- Q_K_MAX) * Q_K1_L) + (np.exp(Q_K2_MAX- Q_K_MAX) * Q_K2_L)
Q_K_SM = np.hstack((Q_K1_SM,Q_K2_SM))
Q_K_SM = Q_K_SM/Q_K_L
Q_K_SM

       [8.07450679e-73, 9.71043646e-67, 1.16778125e-60, 1.40437873e-54],

       [8.19401262e-40, 8.75651076e-27, 9.35762297e-14, 1.00000000e+00]])

Q_K1 =np.vstack((Q1_K1,Q2_K1))
Q_K2 =np.vstack((Q2_K2,Q2_K2))
Q_K = np.hstack((Q_K1,Q_K2))
